The Ministry of Industry's Large Fish Market Will Open Next Spring. The Organizational Law of the Fish Market Has Been Promulgated by Order of the Ministry. 104

Shenshi News Agency reports that in order to relieve the fishing industry, the Ministry of Industry is building a large fish market in Shanghai. Now, all the projects have been completed, and the market directors, etc., are being hired separately. It is expected that it will be officially opened in January next year, but it is still pending the approval of the Ministry of Industry, so the date can be determined. As for the organizational law of the market, the preparatory committee of the fish market had drafted a draft and submitted it to the Ministry. After the Ministry's order, it was changed to the Provisional Regulations on the Organizational Law of the Fish Market. Now, it has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation. The detailed rules and regulations are recorded as follows: "Provisional Regulations on the Organizational Law of the Fish Market of the Ministry of Industry" (1) The Ministry of Industry establishes the Shanghai Fish Market in order to relieve and develop the fish industry in Shanghai. (2) The market is to engage in the entrusted transactions of various kinds of fish, shellfish, and their products within the Shanghai area, and may also transport and sell them independently. Within the Shanghai area, there shall be no other business with the same or similar nature as the market, but this shall not apply to those who have been specially permitted by the market. (3) The first transaction of all fish, shellfish, or their products imported into Shanghai shall be conducted in the market. (4) When necessary, the market may establish branches in the Shanghai area. (5) The market shall have a board of directors, which shall be organized by the Ministry of Industry with the appointment of nine to fifteen directors, with a term of three years. They may be reappointed upon expiration of the term. The board of directors shall have three to five standing directors, who shall be designated by the Ministry of Industry from among the directors, and one person shall be designated as chairman. (6) The market shall have a board of supervisors, which shall be organized by the Ministry of Industry with the appointment of seven to nine supervisors, with a term of three years. They may be reappointed upon expiration of the term. One person shall be designated as chairman by the Ministry of Industry from among the supervisors. (7) The market shall have one manager and two assistant managers, all of whom shall be appointed by the Ministry of Industry, but the manager may also be the chairman of the board of directors. (8) Supervisors may not hold other positions in the market. (9) The manager shall be responsible for all market operations, and the assistant manager shall assist the manager in handling all market operations. When the manager is absent, the assistant manager shall act on behalf of the manager. (10) The following matters shall be executed by the manager after the board of directors has resolved them: (A) Business policy, (B) Budget settlement, (C) Important contracts, (D) Various rules and regulations, (E) Matters proposed by the manager. (11) The functions of the board of directors are as follows: (A) Auditing of accounts, (B) Inspection of business operations, (C) Auditing of budget settlements, (D) Reporting of illegal acts or dereliction of duty by employees. (12) The market shall have the following departments: First Department, Second Department, Third Department, Accounting. (13) The First Department shall be responsible for the following matters: (A) Drafting, receiving, and sending documents and preserving them, (B) Custody of seals, (C) Repair, purchase, and custody of articles, (D) Personnel recruitment, promotion, and performance evaluation, (E) Employment and management of workers, (F) Matters not belonging to other departments. (14) The Second Department shall be responsible for the following matters: (A) Entrusted transactions of fish, shellfish, and their products, (B) Supervision of brokers, (C) Custody and transportation of goods, (D) Management of ships and docks. (15) The Third Department shall be responsible for the following matters: (A) Investigation, statistics, and research on aquatic products, (B) Propaganda, guidance, and publication on aquatic products, (C) Management of machinery, (D) Management of meteorological and signal systems, (E) Management of cold storage and swimming pool operations. (16) The Accounting Office shall be responsible for all accounting matters of the market. (17) The market shall have one secretary, three department heads, one accounting director, two to four technicians, six to nine department members, and two to four technical staff. The secretary, department heads, and technicians shall be appointed by the manager with the consent of the board of directors. The accounting director shall be appointed by the Ministry of Industry, and the remaining staff shall be appointed by the manager and reported to the Ministry of Industry for record. (18) The market may employ assistants, trainees, and employees as appropriate, and the number of staff shall be approved by the Ministry. (19) Each department of the market may set up a deputy director and divide into sections to handle affairs when necessary. (20) When necessary for business operations, the market may hire well-known or experienced people in the fishing industry as consultants. (21) The market shall have brokers who are responsible for purchasing fish, shellfish, and their products on behalf of customers, and the number of brokers shall be determined separately. (22) The market's business regulations and operating rules shall be determined separately. (23) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation."

The Zhabei Charity Group Requests Allocation of Funds for Congee Distribution 105

Distribution will begin on the 25th of this month, and appeals for relief are made to all sectors of society.

The Second Congee Distribution Site of the Zhabei Charity Group on Liuying Road has been in operation for many years. The director of the Zhabei Charity Group, Wang Binyan, presides over it. Every winter, congee is distributed daily to the poor people in various parts of the city, with more than 15,000 people going to eat. Now that the severe winter is approaching again, the group plans to continue distributing congee starting on the 25th of this month and has applied to the Municipal Government and the Social Bureau for an allocation of $2,000. It also appeals to all sectors of society for relief. The original presentation is as follows: "Zhabei is close to the concessions, and laborers and poor people gather here. Every winter, our group has always set up factories to distribute congee. We have now received instruction No. 11920 from the Social Bureau, which states that this year's floods in various provinces are extremely severe, and the countryside is barren. The general public is suffering from disasters, and the poor people who are fleeing famine are flocking to Shanghai. In addition, due to the fatigue of industry and commerce, and the failure of all undertakings, it is difficult for the poor people to obtain food and clothing. The situation this year is special, and it is even more necessary to organize congee distribution. We have been instructed to prepare for congee distribution as soon as possible. We have followed the order and are actively preparing. On the one hand, we have applied to the Municipal Government for an allocation of funds to start the business in order to promote it. At this time of severe weather and sluggish market conditions, the number of unemployed people is large, and the bankruptcy of the countryside is increasing. The large and small factories in Zhabei have not yet recovered, and the silk factories are worried about the lack of raw materials and are mostly closed. The general public is suffering from hunger and cold, which is very pitiful. We have no choice but to follow the order and prepare to distribute congee at the Second Congee Factory on Liuying Road. In addition to instructing craftsmen to repair stoves and houses in advance and to build sheds to protect against rain and snow, we will choose a day to open the business as soon as we have raised a large amount of money. We are specially appealing to all sectors of society, hoping that benevolent gentlemen and ladies will save these hungry and cold people. The merits and virtues are limitless. No matter money, rice, or cotton clothes, please send them to the Accounting Department of our group at Zhongdatong Road, Beidatong Road, Xinzha Bridge. Any little bit of support is welcome. In addition to sending letters to wealthy gentlemen, we will not engage in sporadic fundraising outside. This statement is attached for your public information."

The Common People's Welfare Association's Common People's New Village is Completed 106

Renting will be discussed starting on the 16th of this month, and the heads of each village have been appointed.

The Municipal Committee for the Management of Common People's Welfare Undertakings has added four Common People's New Villages on Qimei Road, Zhongshan Road, Damuqiao Road, and Pushan Road, which have been under construction one after another for several months. Recently, all the projects have been completed, and the association has drafted the Common People's Village Residence Rules and Management Details, which will be submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government for promulgation and implementation immediately. It is reported that the houses in each village include public houses, residences, and dormitories. The residences are divided into two types, A and B. The monthly rent for type A is 3 yuan, the monthly rent for type B is 4 yuan, and the monthly rent for dormitories is 1 yuan. The association has also decided that starting on the 16th of this month, tenants will be allowed to apply for registration directly to the offices in each village, and they can move in on January 1 next year. The houses in each village will also be open for viewing after the 15th of this month. The heads of each village have been appointed and the list is as follows: Hong Xiaonong, head of the Zhongshan Road Common People's Village; Chao Ruisheng, head of the Damuqiao Road Common People's Village; Wang Zufu, head of the Pushan Road Common People's Village; Li Xingnan, head of the Qimei Road Common People's Village. The above heads are all selected from the students with the best performance in the training class of the association and will go to prepare everything in the next few days. The remaining students will be assigned to serve in various villages after the 20th of this month.

Post Office Robbery: Another Accomplice Apprehended 108

Liang Kehe, hiding in Huaian, was arrested and brought back to Shanghai.

The North Sichuan Road Post Office robbery, in which the notorious monk Wukong and his gang used weapons to steal over 90,000 yuan on the morning of September 9th, fatally shooting two and wounding one, was previously reported. Detectives from the Avenue Foch police station went to Funing and other locations in northern Jiangsu, capturing Wukong and several of his accomplices, who were then interrogated and sentenced by the First Special District Court. It has now been learned that another accomplice, Liang Kehe, also known as Liang Ziming, nicknamed “Little Guangdong” or “Little Erzi,” who received 5,000 yuan of the stolen money, has been apprehended. Since the incident, he had been hiding in Huaian, northern Jiangsu. Detectives who originally handled the case learned of his whereabouts and quickly obtained official documents from the First Special Court, secretly traveling to Huaian at night to work with local military and police forces to capture Liang. He was then transported back to Shanghai and brought before Judge Xiao of the First Special Court for interrogation yesterday morning. Zhang Shizhu, the police station's lawyer, briefly described the robbery and Liang's capture, requesting that Liang remain in custody for further investigation. Liang Kehe admitted to participating in the robbery and receiving 5,000 yuan from Wukong. He claimed to have used 2,000 yuan to buy land in his hometown, while the remaining 3,000 yuan was entrusted to his mistress in Shanghai, who later claimed it had been stolen. Judge Xiao ordered Liang Kehe to be detained for further questioning at a later date.

In addition, there is suspicion of inciting murder, and the court issued an arrest warrant. Because the defendant's whereabouts were uncertain, the defendant was not arrested until last night. The police department requested a longer period to investigate the case in detail before filing a lawsuit. People from gambling gangs often came to have fun, and I结怨诬咬阻止因他们吵闹不许到我妓院里来,我麻将亦不懂和数,那裏會做花會因开妓院嘈杂,故于二十二年間盤興別人开设,自己即迁住法华胡家閣,更无叫人杀人之事,我是女流之輩,焉有能力要殺人,亦不知法院要拘捕我,如果我要知道,亦不敢再到上海来了等语. Then the defendant's lawyers stated that they have no objection to the Police Department's request for an extension of the investigation but asked for a shorter time to avoid impeding the defendant's freedom of body, and they demanded that the reform should be shorter and more closely inquired and the Police Department's investigation may be taken. Tibetan Representative Attending Sixth Plenary Session Loses Belongings in Shanghai: 300 Yuan in Cash, 13 Ounces of Saffron, Etc., Stolen. Song Kanbu Sues Andong Hotel for Theft. 113

Song Kanbu, a lama from Sera Monastery in Tibet, was summoned by the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission to attend the Sixth Plenary Session. After the meeting, he took a night express train to Shanghai on the 30th of last month. Upon arriving at the North Station, a greeter from the Andong Hotel at 123 Hubei Road approached him and offered his services. Song followed him by car to the hotel and checked into Room 157. Initially, Song's luggage was stored in the accounting office, but it was later brought to Song's room. As it was late, Song did not open the luggage. The next morning, he discovered that 300 yuan in cash and 13 ounces of saffron brought from Tibet to give to relatives and friends (valued at 60 yuan in Tibet, but worth 300 yuan in Shanghai) were missing. Song believed that he had been very careful along the way and that there was no possibility of losing the items. Therefore, he suspected the hotel. He negotiated with the hotel, and Andong offered to subsidize Song with 60 yuan as travel expenses, but Song refused. He then filed a lawsuit against the hotel with the First Special District Court, accusing them of theft. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Dai Rongduo opened the Ninth Criminal Court for questioning. Yao Yunfang, the hotel's accountant, and Wang Chuanbi, the hotel's lawyer, appeared in court on behalf of Andong. According to Song's statement, the accounting office took a long time to deliver the luggage after he checked into his room, which raised suspicion. Yao Yunfang stated that the hotel could not be held responsible for the loss, as the location of the lost items was unknown. He filed a counterclaim, accusing Song of defamation. Judge Dai reviewed the statements and adjourned the case for further hearing.

Fire on Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Road Kills Three. Wang Shengxing Silk Mill Completely Destroyed. Manager Escapes but is Burned. 114

Yesterday at around 2 AM, a fire broke out at the Wang Shengxing Silk Mill, located at No. 297, Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Road in the South City. The fire spread rapidly, quickly engulfing the roof and spreading to neighboring buildings. Fire brigades from various districts of the South City responded to the alarm, rushing to the scene with pumps to extinguish the fire. The fire was finally extinguished at 3:30 AM. The Wang Shengxing factory and its surrounding structures were completely destroyed. Neighboring structures at No. 295, the Chu Jinji pig bristle workshop, No. 299, the Zhengde Silk Mill, and No. 293, an overpass building, were also affected. When the fire broke out, the workers in the Wang Shengxing factory were fast asleep. When they realized what was happening, they tried to escape, but the stairs had already burned, and the fire was raging. They were trapped by the thick smoke and had no way to escape, ultimately perishing in the fire. The factory manager, engineer Shi Zhijun, managed to escape, but his chest, back, and buttocks were burned. He was transported to Qu Zhibu Hospital for treatment. Firefighters found three charred bodies at the scene, which were unrecognizable. Factory workers identified the deceased as Shi Jixun, 14 years old, the son of Shi Zhijun; Zhang Fengbao, 26 years old, from Chongming; and Yu Qianglang, from Chongming, both workers. The West Gate Branch of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau dispatched police officers to investigate. The local Baochang, Lu Zhaoxiong, was ordered to report the incident to the Shanghai Local Court and request that personnel be sent to the scene for an autopsy. In the afternoon, Public Prosecutor Kong Xianglin and Inspector Shen arrived at the scene to conduct the autopsy. The cause of the fire was said to be due to an electrical fault in the motor inside the Shengxing factory. It was learned that the affected families had large amounts of fire insurance. Wang Shengxing Silk Mill had fire insurance of 1,500 yuan with Zhaotai Bank and 1,500 yuan with Yongning Bank. The Chu Jinji pig bristle brush factory at No. 295 had 5,000 yuan of fire insurance with Yongnian Fire Insurance, and the Zheng Qingji Weaving Factory at No. 299 had 3,000 yuan of fire insurance with Yongning Fire Insurance. The Bureau is currently investigating the matter.

Song Pinshan, a young owner of Song Hengfeng distillery, 29, from Maojia Town Street, Haimen, Jiangsu, seduced Liu Chenshi, a Suzhou woman and the wife of Liu Xiangtai, owner of Liu'an Hotel, who this year turns 35, in the winter of 1933. After having an affair with her, he repeatedly borrowed hundreds of yuan, then defrauded her of gold jewelry valued at 800 yuan. He also seduced her second daughter, Lan Ying, to cohabit. And with Lan Ying, after Lan Ying was abandoned by her brother-in-law, Deng Guihao, who had seduced her and made her pregnant, he caused Lan Ying to file a complaint against Deng Jianhao in the Second Special District Court, resulting in him fraudulently obtaining 8,000 yuan. Later, Liu Chenshi demanded that Song return the borrowed money and jewelry, Song not only ignored her, but took his wife and fled to Shanghai. Liu Chenshi then filed a complaint with the Haimen County Government, accusing Song Pinshan of seduction and inciting murder. The county government approved the suit and summoned him. Song refused to appear, knowing that Song was working as a teacher at Jixian Elementary School on Ganstang Road in the French Concession, the county government transferred the document to the Special District Court, requesting assistance in arresting him, Song then moved to No. 525, Xiude New Village, Chengdu Road, in the Public Concession, which made it impossible to arrest him again. Recently, Liu Chenshi made a special trip to visit Shanghai to find him, and on the 29th of last month, the two met on Xinza Gate Road, where she took Song to the police station and transferred him to the French police station, who transferred him to the Second Special District Court. After Judge Zhang Chaozuo opened the court for questioning, the plaintiff Liu Chenshi requested that the defendant be temporarily detained, pending notification to the Haimen County Government to come and pick him up. Now, she has telegraphed the Haimen County Government to request that someone be sent to pick up the defendant. Yesterday, someone from Haimen came to Shanghai to say that a robbery and murder case had occurred in Xiasha, Haimen, and the county chief went to the countryside to inspect the body. He has public affairs, which are busy and cannot be handled in time. It will take a few days to pick him up. The defendant Song Pinshan stated that the plaintiff said in court last time that I committed fraud, but there is no evidence. I have not committed any fraud. After the court reviewed the statements, it told the police department's lawyer that this court had reviewed the documents from the Haimen County Government. The plaintiff in this case first filed a self-prosecution in Haimen County. The defendant was not present, and no one was found in detention. He asked this court to assist, but he was also unable to arrest the defendant. After verifying that the crime location of the defendant in this case was in Haimen, and the self-prosecution case was in front, this case should be accepted and tried by the Haimen County Government. This court will transfer the defendant to Haimen, what are the opinions of the police department? The police department representative, lawyer Gu Shouxie, replied that the court shall handle it in accordance with the law, and the police department has no objections. Therefore, the court made a ruling in court that this case would not be accepted, and the defendant would be temporarily detained in the detention center, pending the Haimen County Government sending personnel to come and pick him up for interrogation. After the discussion, the court adjourned, and the defendant was taken down and imprisoned in the detention center.

—From Northeast to the Soviet Union—

Mr. Ge Gongzhen was a progressive journalist. His greatest characteristic was his continuous effort and continuous progress. Criminal Case of the Jili Steamboat: Trial of Bandit Gu Jinrong Begins 122

In early June of this year, the Shenhu-line Jili steamboat was robbed by bandits, resulting in a significant loss. Subsequently, Guo Mengshu, the leader of the Northern Station Branch of the Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, along with Qian Tianxiong, Shen Jinchu, and others, apprehended the bandit Gu Jinrong involved in the case. After a clear investigation, the case was prosecuted in the criminal court. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Wu Xiangzu opened the court for the trial. The plaintiff, Wang Zengqing, testified that he was fifty-four years old and worked as an executive in the Silk Industry Association. In June of this year, when the Shenhu-line Jili steamboat arrived at Zhoujiadu, two hundred and nineteen bolts of spun silk, a large amount of silverware, banknotes, and foreign currency were stolen. Seven people, including Li Asheng, had previously been arrested and sentenced to six years in prison. Now, the stolen goods and bandit Gu Jinrong had been apprehended, and he requested that the law be applied. Gu Jinrong, the defendant in custody, testified that he was thirty-something years old, from Songjiang, and worked as a boatman. As for the spun silk and silverware, he claimed that they were purchased with money he had earned from his daily work and denied any robbery, asserting that he had been falsely accused and seeking investigation. Guo Mengshu, the leader of the Detective Team Branch, then appeared in court to recount the circumstances of the arrest. The court appointed lawyer Xue Lisheng to defend the defendant for a long time. He requested that the court call the already-sentenced accomplices to court for cross-examination at the next hearing. The judge granted the request and adjourned the hearing for further proceedings. The defendant was returned to custody.

A Visit to the China Educational Supplies Factory 132

— Jinhua Ting

—Specimens, Models, and Physical and Chemical Instruments—

In recent years, the China Bookstore has been increasingly striving for excellence in its contributions to education, sparing no effort. In addition to extensively inviting scholars and experts to strive to improve textbooks and teaching materials for schools at all levels, it has established the "China Educational Supplies Manufacturing Plant" to engage in the manufacturing of specimens, models, and physical and chemical instruments, in order to supply the education sector nationwide, to facilitate teaching and increase the effectiveness of education. This newspaper believes that the education sector nationwide should have a full understanding of the content of the factory, so it visited the factory the other day. We were grateful for the guidance of Manager Hu Tingmei and the directors of various departments, and we were grateful for the detailed explanations. The establishment process and content and products of each department of the factory are recorded below.

(1) The Process of Establishment

The China Educational Supplies Manufacturing Plant was founded by the China Bookstore. It was established in 1927. The factory site was originally located on Jiayu Road in Hongkou. At that time, it was dedicated to manufacturing specimens and models, which were designated as "China Specimen and Model Factory". In July 1932, "China Instrument Factory" was added to Oujia Road to engage in the manufacture of physical and chemical instruments. Later, due to insufficient production to meet the needs of society, a new factory building was built at No. 721 Zuming Road. By July 1933, the new building was completed, and the two factories were merged. At the same time, efforts were made to expand the scope, and five departments were set up for metalwork, woodwork, paintwork, electroplating, and assembly, to manufacture physical and chemical instruments and educational supplies, and fifteen departments were set up for microscope slides, anatomical injection, collection, insects, combing, peeling, bones, drying, soaking, carving, blank making, writing, coloring, assembly, waxing, and globes, to manufacture specimens and models. At the same time, it was renamed "China Educational Supplies Manufacturing Plant". In April of the following year, a clock-making department was added, dividing the entire factory into three major workshops. Recently, the factory has acquired the house next door to the east and opened it as a botanical garden, with plans to cultivate raw materials for the manufacture of specimens. Since its establishment, it has been eight years, all of which have been managed by Mr. Hu Juntingmei. At present, the factory's equipment is becoming more and more complete, and its products are becoming more and more refined and rapid, enough to supply the needs of educational institutions nationwide.

(2) Content and Organization

The entire factory is divided into three major workshops. Each workshop is equipped with a director and an engineer to plan the various products in the workshop and to supervise the manufacture and research of all the workers in the workshop. The first workshop has more than 100 workers and is divided into five departments, namely (1) the assembly department, which assembles the parts made by other departments into a complete tool; (2) the electroplating department, which electroplates gold or silver on metal tools to make them beautiful, and is currently designing to add lightning-plated chrome equipment; (3) the painting department, which paints various tools or toys; (4) the woodworking department, which uses various woods to manufacture various tools or toys; (5) the metalworking department, which manufactures physical and chemical instruments and tools, most of the machines used in this department are manufactured by themselves, such as the machine for making steel pen plates. The director is Wo Baodi, and the engineer is Wang Weizhi. Mr. Wang is currently the director of the Experimental Workshop of Jiangsu Provincial Educational College and a professor of physics. He is currently designing and manufacturing economic instruments, which will soon be available. The second workshop has more than 100 workers and is divided into fourteen departments, namely collection, insects, plants, microscope slides, peeling, bones, drying, soaking, modeling, blank making, writing, coloring, assembly, and globes. The sole task of this workshop is to manufacture models and specimens. Models are divided into two types: wax and paper. Specimens are divided into two types: system-made and soaked. Among them, the "Microscope Slides Specimens" are the most worthy of our attention. This type of specimen is divided into nine categories: 1. Animals, 2. Plants, 3. Physiology, 4. Fetus, 5. Human Pathology Bacteria, 6. Applied Microbes, 7. Minerals, 8. Rocks, 9. Natural History, with a total of six or seven hundred kinds. Among the nine categories, the most valuable should be human pathological microbes. Because it is extremely dangerous to analyze pathological microbes and manufacture specimens, and if you are not careful, there is a risk to your life, and only China can manufacture this type of microbial glass slides specimen in China, and natural history specimens. It is specially prepared for junior high schools or complete primary schools. The director is Hu Zhenfu, and the engineer is Du Qixi. Mr. Du has a bachelor's degree in biology from Soochow University and is a researcher at Shanghai University. He once served as the editor of the Natural History Department of the Commercial Press. The third workshop has more than 60 workers and is divided into five departments: sampling, metalwork, mold making, assembly and verification. The main work of this workshop is to manufacture monthly, daily, weekly, hour, and minute clocks. The director and engineer is Ruan Shunfa. Mr. Ruan has served as a sampling designer at Xiang Sheng, Hefeng, Old Shipyard, and Zhou Cai Dao Iron Factory. In addition, there are two departments for experimentation and research, so that experimentation and research can be carried out on the main products at any time. The director of the experimental department is Mr. Zheng Zhangcheng, who holds a doctorate in biology from Harvard University and is currently the dean of the School of Science at Shanghai University. The director of the research department is Mr. Ling Wenzhi, who has been the editor of the Natural History Department of the Commercial Press for 22 years.

(3) Main Products

The main products of the factory are roughly as follows: (1) Physical instruments, (2) Chemical instruments, (3) Natural history instruments, (4) Human physiological pathological models, (5) Animal, plant, and mineral specimens models, (6) Microscope slides specimens, (7) Craft specimens, (8) Boy Scout equipment, (9) Various stationery, (10) Monthly, daily, weekly, hour, and minute clocks, (11) Large and small globes, (12) Astronomical instruments, each of the above products is attached with a manual in four languages: Chinese, English, German, and Latin, so that the teaching of schools at all levels can benefit.

(4) Recent Contributions

The factory is rich and determined to be more refined and improve. It never sticks to the old methods for various products. Every time it adds and manufactures, it considers again and again, improves with all its heart, and researches, experiments, and designs new ones, in order to contribute to society. The recent products of the factory are briefly described below: (1) The monthly, daily, weekly, hour, and minute clock does not require constant attention. Just turn on the clockwork, and it can automatically report the month, day, week, hour, and minute. It can run for 22 days and is very accurate. It is the most advanced poem clock in the world. It was invented by Mr. Ruan Shunfa. He devoted himself to research and spent a lot of effort. It took two years to complete. The internal structure of this clock, whether it is the clockwork or the parts, is completely manufactured by itself. It was reviewed and approved by the Ministry of Industry in September this year and approved a ten-year patent. It can produce five units a day and is now officially on sale. (2) Boy Scout Equipment, experts are responsible for guiding the manufacture of all the supplies used for Boy Scout training, and the planning and manufacturing have now been completed. (3) The results of microscopic observation are the most reliable. The factory has added equipment and spent a year, and has now produced various microscope slides specimens, such as animals, plants, minerals, physiology, embryos, and pathogenic bacteria, applied microbes, etc., which were previously sought from foreign countries, but now they should be available in the book. (4) Economic instruments, in order to reduce the difficulty of promoting science education, the factory has specially designed and manufactured economic instruments by Mr. Wang Weizhi. At present, the type A electromagnetic real instrument and the type B first set of physical instruments have been completed. Only the electromagnet of the type A economic instrument electromagnetic experimenter can be used for twelve types of lightning magnetic experiments, such as electric bells, telephones, and telegraphs. The type B economic instrument first set of only 97 pieces can be used for mechanics, heat, and acoustics. There are 678 different experiments, with a thick detailed manual, which will be available soon. (5) Educational toys, in order for schools and families to obtain excellent toys, so that children can play useful games, the factory has also specially designed and manufactured many types of educational toys by Mr. Wang. This type of toy has a beautiful appearance and many changes. Children can play with it for a hundred times without getting tired of it. It is scheduled to be released on New Year's Day next year. (6) Microscope Photography, manufactured by Mr. Zheng Zhangcheng, consultant and director of the experimental department of the factory. Mr. Zheng is currently conducting precise research. According to Mr. Hu Juntingmei, this microscope photography has made considerable progress and will be successful in the near future.

Methods for Donating and Depositing Items at the City Museum 141

Five Commemorative Methods for Donated Items Specified - Deposited Items Must Be Kept for at Least One Year and Cannot Be Retrieved

The Preparatory Office of the City Museum has started collecting exhibits since its establishment. The methods for donating and depositing exhibits are recorded below:

Donation Methods: Shanghai City Museum Donation Regulations: Article 1: These regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 4 of the Museum's regulations for collecting exhibits. Article 2: Items donated to the Museum will be accepted after the Museum agrees. Article 3: For all donated items, in addition to handling according to item A, photos will be printed in a commemorative booklet. (C) For all donated items worth over one thousand yuan, in addition to handling according to item B, the Museum will also present a metal commemorative medal. (D) For all donated items worth over five thousand yuan, in addition to handling according to item C, a display case will be selected and named after the donor. (E) For all donated items worth over ten thousand yuan, in addition to handling according to item C, a display room will be selected and named after the donor. Article 4: For donated items that are extremely valuable and cannot be estimated, or for items whose raw materials are not valuable but require great effort to collect, in addition to registering and marking the facts, the Board of Directors will specially discuss commemorative methods. Article 5: Matters not covered in these regulations may be resolved by the Board of Directors and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and amendment. Article 6: These regulations will be implemented after being resolved by the Board of Directors and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval.

Deposit Methods: Shanghai City Museum Deposit Regulations: Article 1: These regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 5 of the Museum's regulations for collecting exhibits. Article 2: Items deposited in the Museum will be accepted after the Museum agrees. Article 3: The cost of round-trip transportation and packaging of deposited items shall be agreed upon by both parties. Article 4: For all deposited items, the depositor must fill out a deposit certificate in duplicate, one copy to be kept in the Museum for reference, and one copy to be stamped by the Museum and returned to the depositor after the items are collected. The items will be retrieved in the future based on the certificate. Article 5: The deposit period shall be at least one year, unless there are special reasons approved by the Museum. The items may not be retrieved within the period. If the items are not retrieved after the expiration of the period, they will be handled at the Museum's discretion. Article 6: If the Museum believes that deposited items do not need to be displayed or have been displayed for too long and may be damaged, the depositor may be notified to retrieve them at any time. Article 7: If deposited items are not retrieved within three months after being notified by the Museum, or if the deposit period has expired and the items are not retrieved within three years, they will be considered as donated to the Museum. Article 8: After deposited items are formally accepted by the Museum, the Museum shall be responsible for careful safekeeping, except in the event of force majeure such as natural disasters or man-made calamities. Article 9: Matters not covered in these regulations may be resolved by the Board of Directors and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and amendment. Article 10: These regulations will be implemented after being resolved by the Board of Directors and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval.

Tomorrow Afternoon: Completion Ceremony of the National Conservatory of Music's New School Building and Eighth Anniversary Concert 142

The National Conservatory of Music in this city has been in operation for eight years since it was established in 1927. In recent years, it has moved east and west without a fixed location. Since this spring, it has purchased a site behind the Municipal Government on Shijing Road in the city center and started construction. It has now been completed. The completion ceremony will be held at 2:00 PM on the 8th of this month (Sunday), and an eighth-anniversary student concert will be held. Because the school's auditorium has not yet been started due to funding limitations, the meeting will be held in the small auditorium on that day. Guests must be seated with tickets.

Memorial Service for Sun Deqian 143

To be held at Daxia University on December 15th.

Sun Deqian, a senior scholar of Chinese studies, whose style name was Aikang, was known as one of the "Three Gentlemen" along with Wang Guowei and Zhang Er'tian. He was well-versed in classics and history, especially good at philology and parallel prose. His works include more than ten books, such as "Annotations on the Historical Records," "Six Dynasties Parallel Prose," "Essentials of Various Philosophers," and "Brief Examples of Reading Ancient Books," which are profound and refined. German scholar Dr. Yan Fuli and Japanese scholar Fukuda Chiyozo were both his students. The Japanese Ministry of Education once presented his book to the Emperor, which shows the high regard of foreign scholars. He served as a professor at Daxia University for more than seven years. He passed away in Shanghai last month, causing widespread grief. Daxia University has scheduled a memorial service to be held at the school at 2:00 PM on Sunday, December 15th. Condolence messages from all sectors can be sent to the school's administrative office for collection.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (116) 146

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

So they looked up at the glittering stars in the sky, listened to the fragrant grass under their feet, and quietly listened to the chorus of crickets. Robert suddenly said again, "Mommy, Mommy will take a long time to come."

"I don't know why the Creator needs night; isn't daytime much more interesting?" Nan thought to herself.

"It's for people to sleep," Robert replied with a yawn.

"Then go to sleep," Nan said angrily.

"I want my own bed. Ah, I can't wait to see Tanty!" Robert shouted. Hearing the chirping of returning birds in the small nest deepened his longing for home.

"I don't believe your mother will find us," Nan said, feeling anxious and confused. She was impatient for all waiting. "It's so dark here, she won't be able to see us."

"That ice house was pitch black, and I was so scared that I didn't dare to make a sound, but she still saw me; so now, no matter how dark it is, she will always see me," Pan Bo replied with great confidence. At the same time, he stood up and looked into the distance in the dark sky, wondering if there was any news from the savior who had never disappointed him.

"I see her! I see her!" he shouted,勉强dragging his tired little legs and struggling to run towards a slowly moving black shape. Suddenly he stopped, then spun around, stumbled back, and shouted in horror:

"No, it's a bear, a big black bear," he said, hiding his face in Nan's skirt.

Tension in the West Youth Basketball League - Xie Xing Forcefully Defeats McLennan - 41 to 36 - Five Matches Tonight at the Hu 149

The Xie Xing basketball team gathers Fudan athletes and adds the tall and slender Xu Heng as a forward, making it quite strong. In this season's West Youth Basketball League, it won its first match by a large margin against Nanxing. Yesterday, it encountered McLennan for the second time. Relying on its initial momentum, it scored repeatedly and eventually returned triumphantly with a score of 41 to 36, creating a great record of two wins in two battles.

McLennan's Disorganized Lineup

McLennan was originally a top team among the Western teams, with a reputation comparable to that of the Pirates in the past. However, this season, many of its athletes have returned to their home countries, and only a few old players remain, such as Pirelli, Mao Fei, and Levinski. The replacement players have less experience, and the entire team's lineup is disorganized. The team also lacks confidence in throwing baskets, which led to its being at a loss in the first half when facing the agile and brave Xie Xing players. In the second half, the internal connections gradually became more skilled, posing a considerable threat to Xie Xing. However, because of the previous losses, it still lost by five points.

Many Fouls on Both Sides

Due to the intense competition, there were many fouls on both sides. McLennan's Griffis and Xie Xing's Weng Renan, Shu Changge, and Xu Heng were all ejected from the field for four fouls. McLennan's supporters also accused the referee of being unfair, causing a great uproar. In fact, McLennan's players' movements were excessive, both stiff and unclear, and they only blamed the referee after losing.

Xie Xing Gains the Upper Hand First

After the start of the game, Xie Xing gained the upper hand. After McLennan's surrounding basket throw failed, Weng Renan took the lead in scoring. Zhou Dayun wandered under the basket and scored four times, immediately making the score a dazzling 10 to 0. After Weng Renan added another point, McLennan made a major adjustment to its lineup, which indeed led to a turning point. Taonuoer scored a long shot after Xu Heng scored two points. Xie Xing's Zhang Jinxiang also succeeded in a sneak attack, and the score became 18 to 2.

McLennan Follows Closely

After that, McLennan's offense and defense gradually got back on track. "Horse Face" Pirelli scored a hit in front, and Griffis relied on his tall stature to throw in three balls in the back, chasing the score to 10 to 18. The competition became increasingly tense. The Xie Xing athletes, with the determination to break the pot and sink the boat, fought unremittingly. Zhang and Weng, both guards, also launched attacks from time to time while defending, and Qiu Guangxie coordinated in the middle, covering all aspects. Weng Renan was ejected from the field with four fouls. Before long, the whistle sounded, and both sides stopped the game to rest. Xie Xing was ahead with a high score of 27 to 15.

Tense Final Situation

The continuation of the game showed McLennan to be even sharper, but many throws went over the basket and failed to enter. Taonuoer got the ball and mistakenly passed it to Xu Heng, who seized the opportunity to go deep into the basket and scored two points first. Qiu Guangxie then shot successfully from the left side of the field, and the score became 31 to 15. McLennan, seeing the bad situation, worked hard to attack, charging left and right, and frequently fouling. After Pirelli scored three points, he was so eager to steal the ball that he almost had a head-on collision with Xu Heng. Fortunately, Xu knew the importance of forbearance and did not argue with him, so he was able to pass safely. When the score was 36 to 27, Xie Xing's Shu Changge was fined and ejected. The replacement, Li Yunze, had more courage than strategy and became the target of McLennan's attack, chasing the score to 34 to 41, only seven points behind. In a dangerous situation, except for Heng, who was also fined, there were fortunately less than three minutes left. Xie Xing changed from attack to defense, and McLennan failed to achieve its goal. Only Pirelli scored two points. In total, Xie Xing still won by five points.

Observations on the Two Teams' Skills

Looking at the two sides' skills, McLennan's defeat was due to its disorganized lineup and inaccurate basket throws. Xie Xing's victory was due to the entire team's effort, especially Zhang Jinxiang, Zhou Dayun, and Weng Renan, who worked the hardest. However, there were still few changes in tactics, and more research should be done. Then, even if the Pirates are strong, it will not be difficult to achieve the goal and wash away the shame of the Hua team's previous failure.

Letter from Fudan University Cross-Country Team Clarifying the Change of Date for the Jiangnan University Competition 157

A letter from the Fudan University Cross-Country Team states: "Dear Sir, We read in your newspaper's sports column yesterday a letter from the Guanghua Cross-Country Team, which contains many misunderstandings. We hereby provide the following explanation: The Jiangnan University cross-country competition was originally scheduled by the committee to be held at 2:30 PM on November 30th at Jinan University in Zhenru. However, due to heavy rain on that day, it was postponed. According to Mr. Yu Hengzhi, the chairman of the committee, it was proposed to reschedule it to December 4th or 5th. Later, Mr. Peng Wenyu, the director of physical education at Guanghua University, suggested that the 4th would be more appropriate. Therefore, the committee decided to hold it at the same location at 2:30 PM on that afternoon. However, on the evening of the 3rd, Mr. Peng Wenyu of Guanghua raised two reasons to the committee chairman for requesting a change of date: first, because the Chinese Football Association had a match between their school and Youyou on the afternoon of the 4th; second, because the school was holding an exam starting at 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 4th. The committee's view was that it seemed inappropriate for the school to request a change of date because of a match with the Chinese Football Association, as Guanghua was a member of Jiangnan University and should prioritize Jiangnan University. Other competitions should be postponed. As for the school holding an exam, the football team would also not be able to compete. Since the football team had a match, the cross-country team could certainly compete as well. Therefore, the committee did not accept the request. At that time, Mr. Chen Bingde of our school was also present and, seeing that the two sides were unable to reach an agreement, suggested making a slight change to the time to avoid sacrificing studies. The committee chairman then decided to move the event forward to 12:00 noon on the 4th. This is the true story of how the date was changed. The Guanghua Cross-Country Team is unaware that the authority lies with the committee and claims that Fudan did not agree to change the date, which is ridiculous. It should be known that the Jiangnan University Sports Association is organized by various universities, and all issues in various competitions are the responsibility of the committee. Whether or not to change the date is decided by the committee, not by Fudan. Furthermore, the Guanghua Cross-Country Team also stated that it deeply wishes to have a friendly match with our team on any holiday, which is a great honor. Our team only knows that the purpose of the competition is, first, to improve skills, and second, to strengthen relationships. We know nothing else. We are ready to welcome the Guanghua University Cross-Country Team to our school at any time for guidance. We are afraid that the outside world does not understand the truth, so we have sent this special letter. With best wishes, Fudan University Cross-Country Team, December 6th."

Finance: Gold Market Stable and Quiet 159

Fluctuations of Only Two and a Half Yuan; Final Slight Increase of One Dime; Transaction Volume Only 6,000

Yesterday's gold market was generally calm and uneventful due to the quiet overseas gold and silver exchange market. The price fluctuated by only two and a half yuan throughout the day, and trading was very scattered. It is observed that it is difficult to be active before the swap. The morning began with stable overseas silver markets, both in England and America, with forward silver prices in Montreux unchanged or down by up to one li. Exchange rates fluctuated only slightly. London spot gold was unchanged. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with both England and America unchanged. The customs gold unit was unchanged. The standard gold bar price was still listed at 146 yuan and 3 jiao. News of stable exchange rates in Hong Kong's silver market was published in newspapers, slightly stimulating retail investors. The opening was slightly higher, and there was a slight increase after the opening, but sellers took advantage of the high price to sell bars, and the price gradually declined. However, the HSBC exchange rate announcement in the middle of the session, with both England and America unchanged, and the silver balance tax unchanged, resulted in extremely scattered demand and supply. The situation was quite idle, and the fluctuations were very slight. Before long, banks dumped more, and the domestic market became hard. A selling atmosphere suddenly prevailed in the market, and the price continued to decline. Banks took advantage of the low price to cover their positions, and large investors competed to buy at the low price, gradually improving. The forecast for Indian silver was an increase of one anna. The situation at noon remained hesitant. The afternoon market was slightly flat, with buyers slightly active and a slight increase. Trading in the market was even quieter, lacking vitality. The initial report for Indian silver was unchanged, resulting in a stagnant state. The second report for Indian silver was an increase of one anna, and the price slightly decreased, but banks continued to buy cheaply, and the price was maintained after the low. In the end, the market was stable, with only a nine-jiao spread in the after-market, and the situation became boring again. Today's market conditions are recorded below.

The morning opening was 1,145 yuan and 2 jiao, an increase of nine jiao from the previous close. Fuxing, Yongda, and Decheng accepted bars, rising to 5 yuan and 7 jiao. Qingfa, Yonghengchang, and Yongyi Yu divested, falling to 4 yuan and 5 jiao. Meifu made a deal for January US dollars at 4375. Huixiang, Dadecheng, and Hengyu still accepted, rising to 5 yuan and 1 jiao. The HSBC exchange rate announcement, with both England and America unchanged, resulted in a hovering price. Fusheng, Yongyuan, Shengyong Hengyu, Dachangxiang, and Fu Duo sold bars. Shanghai jointly sold US dollars, falling to 4 yuan. Hengyu, Chunyuan, Yonghongkang, and Yong took advantage of the low to maintain, rising to 4 yuan and 5 jiao. The announcement of the silver balance tax being unchanged resulted in Yuanmao Yong, Huixiang Shunmao, Yuxinxiang, Jingfuyingfeng Heng, etc. selling again, falling to 3 yuan and 2 jiao. Zhengjin made a deal for February shillings at 3125. Hengyu, Fuxing, Yongyuan, Changyong, Yongli Chunyuan, and Yonglu were bought, rising back to 4 yuan and 6 jiao. The forecast for Indian silver was an increase of one anna, and the price remained stable. Futai, Yong, etc. slightly supplied. The noon close was 1,144 yuan and 3 jiao, and the price was flat and weak after the close.

The afternoon opening was 1,143 yuan and 9 jiao. Dadecheng Yifeng Yong and Yongli bought in, rising to 4 yuan and 4 jiao. Fuyu and Shunmao slightly sold, and the price fell back to 4 yuan and 1 jiao. The initial telegram from Indian silver was unchanged, and the situation was even flatter. The fluctuations were extremely small, and the transaction volume was also sparse. Wanfeng Qian Changxiang Qian Yuan Yong, etc. slightly sold, falling to within 4 yuan. The second report from Indian silver was an increase of one anna. Jinlong Hengyu and Fuyu sold to 3 yuan and 6 jiao. Yicheng Qingfa Yong Chun Yuan Yong took advantage of the low to buy in, rising back to 4 yuan and 5 jiao. Fuxing Yong took advantage of the high to divest, while Huixiang bought in. After struggling, the noon close was 244 yuan and 4 jiao, and the price was slightly stable after the close.

The settlement price, according to the Central Bank's standard gold bar price, was still listed at 1,146 yuan and 3 jiao. Tinplate Market: Existing Goods are Very Scarce 179

Since the League of Nations imposed economic sanctions on Italy, Italian tinplate has effectively stopped coming to China. As a result, the amount of goods circulating in the market has become scarce. Standard prices have become strong. It is reported that over 300-400 boxes were traded yesterday. It is said that Huacheng, Nanyang, Fujiashing, Meikangyuan and other factories are all adding to their inventory.

Although the harvest of Tianjin red dates is abundant this year, current market prices are already low. Recently, with increased sales, the trend is tightening. High-quality goods have been quoted for around 400 packages. Date heads are priced at 16 to 15.5 yuan, high-quality first-grade red dates are priced at 14 yuan, and third-grade red dates are priced at around 11 yuan, up by varying amounts of four to five jiao.

Daylily Shows a Slight Decline 181

Previously, due to the scarcity of high-quality daylily, medium-grade goods were quoted at 18.12 yuan. The other day, over one hundred packages of high-quality goods were opened, with prices at 18 yuan and 17.8 yuan for the next grade, showing a slight decline compared to before, but there is no expectation of further loosening.

Piece Goods: Cloth Ordering Can Be Said to Have Stopped 182

Worsted wool fabrics have been trading actively, with local traders and those along the Beijing-Hangzhou route continuing to add to their purchases, but mostly in small quantities. Western-style suit fabric sales have been particularly broad. Riding breeches, herringbone patterns, Polish overcoat fabrics, flat thick fabrics, double-sided yellow camel fleece, French West lining horse brown satin, etc., have continued to be produced. However, the ordering business from foreign firms has been very quiet. With foreign exchange and tariffs stalled, importing worsted wool fabrics requires an additional two to three fen. Agents report that the prices still need to be increased, and although the Shanghai market is gradually shouting for higher prices, it is difficult to reach two fen. Furthermore, with rumors rampant in Tianjin, the spring market is difficult to predict. The worsted wool fabric industry has no interest in ordering in the future.

Tidbits 183

— (Rong Yu)

A person who rises from hardship, poverty, and lowliness has two ways of treating people: one is to vent all the anger of his former frustration on the current miserable and lowly people. He thinks that if you don’t accept my anger, you must find a way to rise up like me. This kind of person is inevitably mean and unfeeling, and logically difficult to last. The other is to think about the hardship I suffered in the past, and now in my hands, I will no longer give him hardship. This is extending oneself to others, which is in line with the great path of loyalty and forgiveness. Therefore, I dare to advise people who come from hardship to be kind and not to be jealous and forget their roots.

In this world, as long as one has a strong body, it is a general happiness. If you have a wealth of possessions but are often sick, what is the point? So I changed two ancient poems: "Having strength is enough for everything, being without illness makes one light."

The older one gets, the mind should keep up with the times. If the mind does not keep up with age, then it is "decrepit," "stubborn," and an antique. In Europe, America, Japan, and other powerful countries, their rulers, business leaders, university professors, etc., although old, their minds are still a progressive and active youth, so they can do things with such results.

Before Life and After Death 184

— Chen Liang

Xianggen is dead! This news came from the mouth of another old school janitor.

A middle-aged woman with a white headband on her bun, leading a child wearing a plain hat, always holding two seemingly frozen tears, went in and out of the gatehouse.

The male students' argument: "Who told him to eat two dumplings, four taels of eggplant skin wine, and spoil his stomach!"

The female students' argument: "A woman whose husband dies should wear hemp, but Xianggen's woman only wears a white headband, which is too inappropriate!"

No one at the school authority mentioned Xianggen's aftermath. It is said that the body is still lying on the board without a coffin for burial. It seems that his death has nothing to do with everyone and is less regrettable and noticeable than the death of a monkey in the zoo. There is also a reason for this: Xiang Xian'gen had no good feelings for him when he was alive.

It is often heard that people rebuke him:

"Borrow money, borrow money, the previous one hasn't been paid back, and now you're opening your mouth again. You just go play the lottery, drink, gamble, and have fun, as if someone owes you. You're really too shameless. What about your monthly salary? You're really a muddlehead, a bastard. To be honest, I won't lend you next time..."

Once he also opened his mouth to me. He hoped that I would get first place and a scholarship. However, I still disappointed him after all. I didn't have any money, and he was naturally disappointed, and I was also uneasy. Five days later, he got sick and died. It was still the faculty who had a bit of compassion and randomly donated dozens of dollars to his wife for the funeral.

"You also give a little bit, for example... he borrowed bits and pieces from you when he was alive." Another old janitor earnestly pleaded with the male and female students and also raised dozens of dollars. The old janitor led the woman with the white headband in to thank him. A look of black worry appeared on his forehead:

"Xianggen is dead, and someone will take care of him, what about myself, I...?" His mouth twitched.

Record of the Tianquange Fine Arts Exhibition 185

— By Ear

The Tianquange Calligraphy, Painting, Inkstone, and Fan Exhibition, which has been brewing for a long time, opened on the 29th at the Lake Society and is scheduled for seven days. Today is the last day. I have visited it for several days. The first day was purely for calligraphy and painting, and on the second and third days, inkstones and fans were added, which were dazzling and beautiful. The most noteworthy were the Song and Yuan collection handscrolls, which were collected by Mr. Qian Zeshi. Xia Taichang's "Wind and Rain Bamboo" had many inscriptions by his contemporaries. Sheng Zizhao's "Jiangtian Fishing Music Picture" is also a memorable work. Chou Shifu's imitation of Liu Songnian's "Autumn Crossing Picture," a small green and blue landscape hanging scroll, has Qianlong's jade seal and Liang Jiaolin's collection seal on it. This is genuine, and Chou's craftsmanship is very impressive. It is not something that ordinary weak and stagnant works can compare to. What is particularly awe-inspiring is Fang Zhengxue's rubbing of Yan Lugong's "Magu Immortal Altar Record," with a postscript by Hai Gangfeng. Loyal and virtuous cooperation can be called a triple perfection. Among the fans, there were ten small fans from the Inner Court, painted by Tang Dai and written by Zhang Ruoxia, which were exquisitely beautiful. There were also more than one hundred Xiangfei bamboo bone fans of various sizes. Among the inkstones, there were ceramic inkstones handmade by Gao Nanfu and Zhao Wenmin's "Song Xue Qi Chen Ni Inkstone." On that day, the number of visitors reached thousands. In the afternoon, Guizhou Road was crowded with traffic. Buyers were from the financial sector, such as Xu Jiqing, Shen Laiqing, Qu Jigang, Qin Yingchun, Shen Jixuan, and Zhou Shouliang. Those in the literary and artistic circles, such as Li Yaoke, Zhou Jianyun, Mei Lanfang, and Liu Haisu, and collectors such as Ye Yuhu and Zhang Congyu, were particularly enthusiastic. The famous painter Feng Chaoran also came to the meeting to select countless fine works. I asked the owner about this, and he said that it was the gold tycoon Wang Boyuan who invited them to choose. Zhang Weirush bought several fans worth a fortune, which was also a heroic act. I feel that our country's culture and art urgently need to be promoted, so I write this to inform those who care about art. The impact on the world after the opening of the London exhibition was great and significant, but our people were indifferent. If the powerful did not promote it, it would be laughable to foreigners.
