Short Story

Crab Stories 189

— Wu Yafei

Twenty years ago, perhaps on a mid-September evening, we were gathered around a kerosene lamp eating lake crabs. My father suddenly put down the crab he was eating, wiped his eyes with the back of his hand, his face filled with such dejection and sorrow, his eyes moist. We were all surprised and suspicious, and no one dared to put another crab in their mouths. But father finally told a crab story in a faint voice, and as he spoke, he was weeping: (What follows is a tragic tale my father told my mother)

"Although it was twenty years ago, I still remember it very clearly, almost as if it were yesterday: Now when I eat crab, I think of this matter, and at the same time I think of the irreconcilable murderer of my father - he is now the administrative commissioner of my hometown, holding all the authority in the village, ×××. Although I have thought about avenging my father, I hate that I am also a weakling, so I have never had the courage to do so: Now I watch my enemy swaggering around, oppressing the people in my hometown. But myself? Still a wanderer in a strange land... But every time I see or eat crab, every time I think of my father's tragic death, and at the same time I think of the pomp and power of the murderer, besides crying at home, or secretly shedding a few tears, I can only feel ashamed, curse my own fate, and resent myself for being so useless!"

"My father died for crabs, and I myself have wandered here because of crabs, becoming a person who can never return home!"

"Originally, we were a fishing family, and had not changed our profession for generations, just making a living by the water. My family had two fish ponds, two fishing boats, and more than ten acres of floating reeds. Besides my father working as a fisherman all year round, sometimes my mother and sisters would also help to row the boat and cast the net. I was still young at that time, so I just stayed at home to look after my younger brother."

"The fishing season was during the Major Production Festival, only one winter each year. Our life during the year depended on the harvest of this winter. The sporadic catches at ordinary times, such as catching shrimp and crabs, could only be used to supplement our daily expenses. However, in our area, whether it was fish, shrimp or crabs, there were often people who came to steal them from the ponds, so even in the middle of the night, we had to go out to patrol to see if there were any thieves. Moreover, at that time, there was a ××× who specially hired several people to steal fish in this fishing village. He had great power, so although everyone hated him with all their teeth, no one dared to do anything to him. Everyone only gave him a nickname "King of Fish Thieves" behind his back."

"Only my father often went to confront him, so he hated my father almost to the bone."

"One day - it was the beginning of September, when lake crabs should be on the market, so my father went to catch crabs and check the fish seedlings in the pond as usual every night. But when my father got near the reeds, he saw two dark figures quickly darting into the reed clumps: My father was quick-witted and chased after them and caught one of them, while one escaped. My father threw him into the mud, forcing him to say who had instigated him to steal. He knelt on the ground begging, and told my father everything, and returned all the stolen crabs to my father. My father was satisfied and let him go back."

"The next day, my father went as usual, but he didn't come back until after dusk. He knocked weakly on the door, coughing and groaning. My mother opened the door and helped him to the bed. I only saw him covered in mud, holding his heart with his hand, constantly spitting out blood. Many places were covered in blood. When he took off his clothes, there were patches and strips of wounds on his body! My mother was so anxious, crying and shouting, asking him what had happened. He finally told her everything from beginning to end, and said:

""These people were sent by ×××, my enemy is ×××""

"My father died of overwork a week later, so my mother took me and carried my younger brother to the yamen to complain, but they were ultimately powerful, so it ended without result due to insufficient evidence."

"From then on, my mother worked hard to raise us, selling all the fish products to provide for our lives and education. She said:

""Children, throw away this bowl of bitter rice. You'll die of heat in the summer and freeze to death in the winter. Your father lost his life to a strongman for this bowl of rice. You should change your profession!""

"So, we embarked on this path of life."

My father was already sobbing as he spoke, so we also shed tears as we looked at the big pile of crabs on the table, and my mother was heartbroken and sobbing!

Now, every time I see those live, crawling crabs in the wire knots and flower pots, it seems that every one of their feet is scratching and crawling on my heart, making my heart sad, and finally I can't help but think of the tragedy my father described—

My father told this story twenty years later, and it happens that I am writing this novel twenty years later. Calculating it, it has been more than forty years since the tragedy occurred!

Adjustment and Calibration Steps for Superheterodyne Receivers 190

— Fuping

The adjustment circuit of a superheterodyne radio is the most complex. The natural frequencies of each stage are not completely the same as those of adjusting a tuned radio frequency (TRF) receiver. Therefore, at first, this type of radio was difficult for ordinary people to use, except for a few trained technicians. Since the invention of single-knob tuning, most tuning capacitors are installed on a single shaft, so as long as a dial is turned to any point, the tuning circuits of each stage of the radio are precisely matched. Factory-made radios are, of course, carefully inspected before leaving the factory, but afterward, they are unfortunately subjected to strong vibrations, or the user carelessly tampers with the calibrated compensation capacitors and intermediate frequency (IF) amplifier tuning capacitors, causing confusion. Although all the components of the radio are not damaged at all, its entire fate has been ruined. Unless there are sophisticated instruments and experienced technicians, it is difficult to restore its original glory. How to re-calibrate a superheterodyne radio that has been disrupted is indeed some practical knowledge that we amateur researchers must know.

The necessary instrument for calibrating a superheterodyne receiver is an accurate test oscillator (it must at least include the intermediate frequency and broadcast band). Its manufacturing method has been described many times in this publication, so there is no need to repeat it. Now let's start talking about how to use this test oscillator to calibrate a superheterodyne receiver.

The first step to calibrate is the IF amplifier tuning circuit. The most common frequency for the IF amplifier is 175 kHz, but there are also other frequencies such as 465 kHz. These are noted on the back of the radio or in the instruction manual. If the IF amplifier has changed from its original frequency, the symptoms are like poor selectivity, squealing heterodyne, and repeat points. For the calibration method, first match the frequency of the test oscillator so that it is exactly equal to the intermediate frequency specified for the radio. Remove the oscillator vacuum tube from the radio and connect the "antenna" end of the test oscillator output to the control grid of the IF amplifier tube (if there is more than one stage in the IF amplifier, start calibrating from the last stage first). Modern radios mostly use screen grid tubes for the IF amplifier, so connecting to the control grid only requires touching the copper cap on top of the vacuum tube: Connect the "ground" end of the test oscillator (usually the isolated case of the oscillator) to the cathode of the IF amplifier tube. Turn on the radio. At this time, the speaker should emit a squealing sound. The test oscillator is best to use already amplitude-modulated (AM). Otherwise, the IF amplifier stage of the radio must be oscillated first. Use a small screwdriver with an insulating paper layer on the iron rod to prevent short circuit danger from touching the chassis. Insert it into the IF amplifier transformer and rotate the adjustment screw of its secondary tuning capacitor, paying attention to the volume emitted by the speaker, and rotating it to the loudest level. It would be more accurate to use an "output meter" instead of a speaker to indicate. Repeat the same method to calibrate the previous stage IF amplifier, making sure that the entire IF amplifier section completely matches the specified frequency.

After the IF amplifier stage is calibrated, the next step is the oscillator stage, which is also the most important point in the entire process. Now the removed oscillator tube can be inserted. Connect the "antenna" and "ground" terminals of the test oscillator to the "antenna" and "ground" terminals of the radio, respectively. Set the test oscillator to the high-frequency end of the broadcast band, for example, 1480 kHz, and then change the capacity of the compensation capacitor attached to the oscillator stage tuning capacitor until the maximum output is obtained. At the same time, the test oscillator must be tested with several frequencies in the broadcast band, because the frequency difference between the oscillator stage and the high-frequency amplifier and the first detector stage may not be able to maintain the intermediate frequency at any point on the radio scale. If the numbers indicated on the radio dial are the calibrated frequency numbers, it will be of great help when calibrating the oscillator stage. We only need to pay attention to whether the frequency indicated on the dial is the same as the test oscillator when the radio output is maximum, and we can determine whether the compensation capacitor of the radio oscillator stage has been calibrated.

The high-frequency amplifier stage and the first detector stage are the last step, which is relatively the easiest, and the method is the same as calibrating a TRF radio. Just match the natural frequencies of each stage tuning circuit to be the same as the input signal frequency, and the speaker or output meter will indicate the maximum output. This completes the entire calibration process.

If we do not have an expensive "output meter", we can also use a milliammeter to replace it. Connect a 0-5 milliammeter to the plate circuit of the second detector tube. If the detection system uses the grid negative voltage method (usually called plate detection), the plate current indicated by the milliammeter is also the largest when the radio output is maximum. If the detection system uses the grid leak capacitor method (usually called grid detection), the index of the detector tube plate current is the smallest when the output is maximum.

Shortwave Radio Using a Single Coil 191

— Jian

The shortwave radio to be introduced in this article is one that can receive various shortwave bands using only one coil. The diagram below shows the circuit of the radio. Because its structure is quite simple, it is very suitable for beginners to make. The values ​​of each part are detailed in the diagram, so there is no need to repeat them here. Here, I will only tell readers how to make the coil:

Take a cylinder with a diameter of one inch and a length of three inches, and wind ten turns of No. 26 double silk-wrapped wire at a distance of half an inch from one end. This is L1 shown in the diagram. The winding head should be connected to the grid of the detector tube, and the winding tail should be connected to the first tap. Next, wind seven turns at about half an inch away to form LN, with the winding head connected to the first tap and the winding tail connected to the second tap. Then wind 24 turns again at a distance of half an inch to form L3, and after connecting to the second tap, wind one turn in the opposite direction to form L5. L4 is formed by winding three turns in the middle of L1 and L2, with the winding head connected to the choke coil and the winding tail connected to the plate of the detector tube. Except for L5, all coils are wound in the same direction, and the winding method is close winding.

When using a variable capacitor with a value of 25 uuf (maximum) and 100uf (minimum), the wavelength range that can be received: 16528 m for L1, 25S38M for L1L2, and 45S55M for L1L2L3.

The regenerative (or feedback) coil includes L4 and L5. This is the most special point of this machine. If this regenerative coil is changed to one, that is, if the number of turns is reduced to make it oscillate at a shorter wavelength, it will not oscillate at a longer wavelength. If the number of turns is increased, the oscillation at a shorter wavelength is too strong, so the screen grid voltage in the detector tube must be reduced, and the sensitivity is reduced. Therefore, it is impractical to use only one regenerative coil. To solve this problem, two regenerative coils are used. When using L1 or L1L2 to receive radio, only L4 has feedback effect. When using L1L2L3 to receive radio, L4 and L4 simultaneously act as regenerative coils to provide feedback.

The Impact of Constellations on Radio Waves (Continued) 192

— Jue Ming

3. The Impact of Meteor Showers on Radio Waves

In 1921, while Mr. Bickel was experimenting with 800-cycle radio waves, he saw a large meteor, and at the same time the radio emitted a lot of noise, so he presumed that this noise was caused by the radio waves being affected by the meteor. On the other hand, Dr. Nagaoka of Japan also made the same discovery.

So what is the impact of these meteors and meteor showers on radio waves? According to the research of Dr. Nagaoka of Japan, he excluded all other factors that could affect the radio waves when the Earth passed through the meteor shower, and focused on studying the impact of meteors, measuring the reception intensity. The result is shown in the first figure.

(1) The impact of meteors on radio waves is shown in Figure 1A. O in the figure is the day with the most meteors, in other words, the time of passing through the central part of the meteor shower. Sixty days before this day O with the most meteors, the radio waves had already been affected and changed. This impact reached its peak 18 days after the day O with the most meteors. Sixty days later, the impact had not completely disappeared.

(2) However, if we talk about ordinary meteor showers in general, the fluctuations in their impact are somewhat different. Usually, as shown in Figure 1B, the radio waves have been affected and changed 60 days before the day O with the most meteors. The impact reaches its peak 22 days after the day O with the most meteors. The impact begins to disappear 80 days later.

(3) Conversely, if receiving signals from Nauen, Germany, across the Atlantic Ocean, the impact is exactly the opposite of the above two examples. These signals become weaker due to the impact of meteor showers. This impact appears 60 days before the day O with the most meteors. The impact is strongest a few days before and after the day O with the most meteors. It begins to disappear 80 days after the day O with the most meteors, as shown in Figure 1C.

4. The Impact of Constellations on Radio Waves

The impact of meteors and meteor showers on radio waves has been described above, so what is the relationship between ordinary constellations and radio waves?

The fact that constellations can affect radio wave communication was only discovered last year by Mr. Jansky, an engineer at Bell Telephone Company.

One day, while he was experimenting with a very long antenna and a short wave of 1.46 meters, he heard a lot of noise. In order to study the source of this noise, he changed the direction of the antenna in various ways, and as a result, he knew that the noise was the strongest when the antenna was facing a certain direction. The direction of this strongest noise was changing every day, and gradually became weaker and then stronger again. After a full year, in other words, on the day exactly one year after the discovery of this noise, the direction and strength of the noise were the same as when it was discovered a year ago (the change in direction during the year is shown in Figure 2). Therefore, he presumed that this cause was outside the Earth, and studied the direction with the greatest impact. As a result, astronomy knew that this direction was exactly the center of the Milky Way. Combining the above facts, he believed that for various reasons, the Milky Way could broadcast a kind of radio wave back to Earth: this is the source of the noise in his experiment.

In the current wireless academic community, although it is not yet possible to say definitively whether the Milky Way can emit radio waves to the Earth, it cannot be denied that it can have a great impact on radio waves. (End)

Small experience

Simple Test Method for Small Fixed Capacitors 193

— Yong Yan

Equipment: One 45-volt B battery, one pair of high-quality earphones.

Test method: Connect the positive and negative terminals of the 45-volt B battery to the two wiring terminals of the small fixed capacitor to be tested, and charge it for about one or two seconds. Then remove the battery, and then connect one terminal of the earphones to the two wiring terminals of the capacitor, and carefully listen to the sound in the earphones.

Judgment of good or bad: If a loud "ka-ka" sound is heard in the earphones, it indicates that the capacitor is intact and usable; if the sound is faint or completely silent, it indicates that it is leaking, short-circuited, or the connection line is broken. In other words, it is not applicable.

Mr. Cao Runsheng, please provide another seal.

Sincerely,

A Case of Curing Weakness and Illness 197

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essays

The Education Bureau Cares About the Improvement of Drama 205

— Mengruo

Drama is a form of social education, and its impact on the public is significant. Good drama can leave a good impression on the audience, while bad drama can harm society. However, all dramas in our country are either immature (new ones), or the old ones not only fail to meet the goals of social education but also carry a strong feudal color or hinder public morals. Recently, the Municipal Education Bureau has been determined to improve various dramas. Previously, seeing the influence of comedic skits deeply rooted in the people, and in order to use them as a powerful tool for promoting social education, the bureau specially assigned members of the Drama and Record Review Committee to lead the city's stand-up comedians and organize the Shanghai Stand-up Comedy Research Association. This will not only enhance the social status of stand-up comedians but also enable all performers to earnestly improve their lyrics in order to achieve a subtle and transformative effect. The results have been very good. Stand-up comedies that used to sing about the incompetence of crying kings are now able to spread social education. Recently, the association's seventh regular meeting decided on six concrete measures to improve stand-up comedy. In the passive aspect, there are four prohibitions: (1) No indecent words or performances are allowed, (2) No abusive sentences are allowed, (3) No mourning tunes are allowed, (4) No lyrics and performances that have been banned by the authorities are allowed. In the active aspect, there are two requirements: (1) All members, whether performing in theaters or broadcasting on the radio, must insert a section of lyrics that is beneficial to society and contains educational meaning into each performance, (2) All members must copy the lyrics completely and submit them to the Education Bureau for review. This phenomenon is very gratifying.

Recently, the Education Bureau, considering that the "bengbeng" operas being performed by Bai Yushuang and others at the Empire Theater and the North China Opera Theater were filled with obscene singing and gestures, specially sent reviewers to the theaters to review them and gave them separate bans and improvements. And a few days ago, they gathered all the actors and talked to them at the Civic Education Hall, explaining the social education mission undertaken by the drama, and pointed out the points that should be improved: (1) In terms of tone, there should be no obscene puns, (2) In terms of sound, there should be no decadent music, (3) The action should not be dirty, (4) Horror plots are prohibited, (5) Actors should not have actions that tempt the audience, (6) The insertion of stage scenes should not be exaggerated too much. These points should not only be improved in "bengbeng" opera, but also in other dramas.

The Municipal Education Bureau's recent implementation of drama improvement to assist the promotion of social education is commendable. Especially this time, the handling of "bengbeng" opera does not take the means of strict prohibition, but sends personnel to review it in order to determine the improvement, which is quite able to take care of the livelihood of the actors. However, we still have some opinions on the improvement of old dramas in our country. It is true that drama is a kind of social education. But why can bad dramas be produced in our society? And why do the general public like to watch these kinds of bad dramas? We hope that the education authorities in our country can also pay close attention to these two questions.

Singing the News (Continued) 206

— Xinye

"The countryside is really dead. After dark, you can't take a step except to sleep!" It was indeed a youth who was obsessed with city life, and being back in his hometown for only half a month made him feel depressed.

"Why don't you go to the teahouse in town?" the young aunt said faintly, glancing at her mother.

"I don't like going to that kind of dirty and vulgar place!" He yawned, seeming a little tired.

"Go to sleep!" The third aunt, who was making shoe soles for the child, also opened her mouth.

There were seven of us together, but besides the third aunt making shoes, the young aunt knitting a woolen sweater, and me reading a novel, there were four other people sitting idly in their corners, casting their eyes on the dim flames, but the flames did not understand, only being fanned by the wind blowing in from the window, flickering. The lamp flowers, one by one, were stacked up like embroidered hydrangea balls.

The village dog was barking frantically, and the old hen in the chicken coop was awakened from her sweet dreams, clucking loudly. Xiong and Ying had stopped talking, and were all silent. I also put down the book I was reading and listened attentively...

"Dong dong! Dang... dong dong! Dang!" The sound of someone beating a leather drum and small gong gradually approached from afar and finally reached the front of our house. In the past, we often heard this sound at dusk, but because everyone was playing mahjong or engaged in other exciting games, no one would pay attention to it, but today, every beat seemed to strike in the hearts of each of us; the sound was particularly harsh.

"It's the news singer. Let's call him in to sing the news!" Xiong seemed to have discovered something and jumped up happily.

Goddess 207

— Jiang Mi

An old peasant who had escaped from the war zone sat like a wooden chicken at the foot of Buzhou Mountain, his face showing infinite resentment. He had used up his sweat and blood to irrigate the rice in his fields, which was now more than a foot high, but a declaration of war trampled on his fields, destroyed his houses, and even caused his wife and children to be scattered. He wondered when the water of the Yellow River would clear and when the world could be peaceful? (9)

Page 19

The news singer was a blind man in his forties and a little girl of twelve or thirteen. The blind man held a broken huqin in his right hand, but a five- or six-foot-long dry tobacco pipe in his left. The little girl also held the copper bowl of the dry tobacco pipe in one hand and a drumstick in the other. Around her neck hung a small leather drum and a small gong, hanging straight in front of her chest. It seemed that they were father and daughter. He sat down in the hall, loaded a pipe with tobacco and smoked it, waiting for our words, but the little girl searched everyone's faces with her two not very clever eyes, as if to discover some miracle.

The blind man smoked for a while, knocked the head of the pipe twice on the square brick, knocked off the ash, then picked up the broken skin huqin, tightened the strings, and corrected the sound.

As he pulled and sang, we were all quiet, listening with our heads tilted. Everyone stared at the blind man's face, but there was not a trace of expression on his face; his face was waxen yellow, his nose was flat, only two thin lips were mechanically moving, and a mouthful of scorched yellow and defective teeth often showed from that crack.

The blind man finished singing the news, collected the money, and when he was leaving, he said "Thank you!" to us. In the distance, the second watch had been lightly struck! (The End)

— Laoxin

(I love to watch the eagle soaring in the sky, and I love to listen to his clear singing even more! Young friends, don't forget: what he tells us!)

Not forgotten, not forgotten at all. Not forgotten the clear singing of the great eagle, nor forgotten the singing of the friend who soared like an eagle. Their clear and crisp singing, like the bugle call that inspires everyone's courage, sings the sharp and majestic melody non-stop, without end, exciting me, leaping into the hearts of every young person.

It was an evening. In that distant south, we, a group of young children, had a very simple gathering. We were sighing, our eyebrows knotted in silence, not saying a word. The sun stubbornly poked its head out from the foot of the western mountains, with a little pity, its face flushed, and looked angrily. Darkness, revealing a ferocious smile, opened a large black curtain, covering the whole earth in a gray and terrifying world. The four of us leaned against a cliff, two weeping, one sighing, and one shouting angrily and rudely. To the end, there was only a desert left, the desert shut its mouth; the young man also shut his mouth, lowered his head, and supported his chin with his strong hand, not saying a word. The Grand Occasion of "Beware of Pity" in Paris 215

The detective masterpiece "Beware of Pity," which shocked the world and is known to everyone, young and old, was released at the Paris Grand Theater on Avenue Joffre yesterday. The box office success is unprecedented, which shows the greatness of the film. Those who have seen it should see it again, and those who have not seen it should not miss this last chance.

The Play Within a Play in "Flower of Spring" 216

Interesting Facts on the Set

"In 'Flower of Spring,' there are several sketching shots in the photography. Gao Zhanfei is hired by a film company as a temporary actor in the play to replace a male lead in a diving scene because his face is similar to that of the male lead. At the same time, because of his financial problems, he had no choice but to take the dangerous dive that others were unwilling to try.

Here, Wu Cun, the director of 'Flower of Spring,' uses these shots to satirize the current noble and corrupt film practitioners. When the heroine, Zhu Qiuhen, comes out of the dressing room, singing a foreign film song, she walks to Gao Zhanfei, greets him, and gives him candy. At this time, the old Gao, who was hired as a temporary actor, is very surprised by the heroine's kind gesture. Zhu Qiuhen suddenly feels that the button on her clothes is not buttoned properly and coquettishly asks Gao Zhanfei to button it for her.

Suddenly, a real male lead runs out of the production department, walks up to Zhu, and shouts, "Hey! Miss Zhu, what are you doing?"

Zhu Qiuhen is greatly surprised to see the male lead: "Ah! Aren't you here? Who are you?"

Male lead: "He is a temporary actor and will replace me in the diving scene."

It turned out that Zhu Qiuhen mistook Gao Zhanfei for her beloved male star, resulting in such a joke.

Recent News from the Yangtze River Theater Company 217

Since its establishment, the Yangtze River Theater Company has been actively working and all items are ready. The first public performance was originally planned to be Moliere's "The Hypocrite" or Messfield's "The Tragedy of the Fair Penitent". After several discussions, it was decided to change Roman Rolland's "The Game of Love and Death" and Moliere's "The Imaginary Invalid" into the scripts for the first and second public performances.

A Scene from Bu Wancang's "Triumphant Song" 218

Silver Jottings 219

— Zhi Er

The promotion of "Hero of the Times", "The evil spirit shouts for Gary Cooper." In addition to being extremely busy, Gong Zhifang's wife, Miss Shen Yiyun, also practiced the husband-sings-wife-follows, as evidenced by Miss "Yiyun's" promotional manuscript for "Hero of the Times" in yesterday's Film Times.

The Times reported: "The humble person says! Tianyi is a great base for cultivating talents. Hu Die, Shen Xiling, and Lu Xiaoluo, which one of them did not come from our Tianyi?"

Nine-tenths of "Tianlun" will be shown at "Great Light" (nine-tenths, because there are still problems with Jin Cheng), but the date is two days

After "Boat Girl," "Hero of the Times" will be shown, and the date will be next Thursday. The long-rumored "Peach Blossom Dream" will have to be postponed again.

The promotional manuscript for "Peach Blossom Dream," directed by Dan Duyu, who is known for his sensuality, says: "Dan Duyu, who has progressive ideas, once said that the film is in a leading position, so it should not cater to the general low-level audience, and should do its best in art..."

Reading it is like sitting comfortably on a sofa chair.

The John Theater Company performed "Just Returned," "Two Friends in Need," and "The Fall" last night.

Li Amao's daughter, Ms. Xu Qi, will marry Sun Xiang on the water today. This is a major film event in 1935, this is a record.
